goULFa"><span>The wide-ranging investigation into Donald Trump's business activities and ties to Russia began with a protocol-breaking interview with Alexander Downer.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>The former Foreign Minister and then High Commissioner to the United Kingdom spoke to the FBI in the </span><a href="https://www.9news.com.au/national/2017/12/31/11/14/alexander-downer-russia-revelations-raise-questions-for-australia-s-relationship-to-white-house"><span>first few days of the investigation</span></a><span>, the </span><em><span>New York Times</span></em><span> reports.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>Downer was granted permission from Canberra to break diplomatic protocol to be interviewed by agents in London in August 2016.</span></div></div><div><div id="adspot-mobile-medium"></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>Downer spoke with the FBI about a conversation he had at a London wine bar with </span><a href="https://www.9news.com.au/world/2017/10/31/06/45/who-is-george-papadopoulos-campaign-advisor-guilty-plea-donald-trump-russia-collusion"><span>Trump campaign adviser George Papadopoulos</span></a><span> that May.</span></div></div><figure class="article__image"><img alt="Alexander Downer (second from left), with Malcolm Turnbull, Prince Harry, Meghan Markle and Lucy (AAP)<!-- --> <!-- -->(AAP)</figcaption></figure><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>Papadopoulos purportedly told Downer that Russia had accessed thousands of embarrassing emails sent by </span><a href="https://honey.nine.com.au/2018/05/12/09/15/hillary-clinton-sydney-event"><span>Hillary Clinton</span></a><span>.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>When those emails started being released by Wikileaks, Australian officials contacted their American counterparts, triggering the FBI investigation initially named Crossfire Hurricane.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>Crossfire Hurricane is a phrase from the Rolling Stones song 'Jumping Jack Flash'.</span></div></div><div><div class="OUTBRAIN" data-reactroot="" data-src="//www.9news.com.au/world/crossfire-hurricane-trump-russia-investigation-started-with-alexander-downer-interview/16121e23-bdfc-4f32-9822-e4a7f841e3e4" data-widget-id="AR_5"></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>Papadopoulos has pleaded guilty to lying to the FBI and is now a cooperating witness in the special investigation.</span></div></div><figure class="article__image"><img alt="George Papadopoulos (third from left) in a meeting with Donald Trump. (Instagram)<!-- --> <!-- -->(Instagram)</figcaption></figure><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span> </span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><strong><span>Double standards</span></strong></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>As it is revealed how much the FBI knew before the election, the bureau is facing increasing criticism for staying silent.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>FBI Director James Comey breached protocol by announcing they had reopened an investigation into Hillary Clinton's emails.</span></div></div><figure class="article__image"><img alt="Hillary Clinton at a rally in Orlando, Florida. (AP)</figcaption></figure><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>Clinton has said the announcement, made a week before the election, cost her the presidency.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>"I have laid out in I think very persuasive evidence that (Comey's) intervention on October 28 was the most important reason why I ended up losing 11 days later," Clinton said.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>The investigation was closed days later with no wrongdoing found.</span></div></div><div class="block-content"><div class="styles__Container-sc-1ylecsg-0 goULFa"><span>Meanwhile, the FBI was in a more serious, deeper investigation of then-candidate Donald Trump and his associates.</span></div></div><figure class="article__image"><img alt="Former FBI Director James Comey testifies in front of the Senate Intelligence Committee.
